Inside main or user-defined function

   (get_local $sp)

  (set_local $$1

  )
  (set_local $$2
   (i32.load
    (i32.const 1536)
   )
  )
  (set_local $$3
   (call $_vfscanf
    (get_local $$2)
    (get_local $$0)
    (get_local $$1)
   )
  )
  (return
   (get_local $$3)
  )
 )
